# <a name="obsolete-types-in-the-net-framework"></a><span data-ttu-id="e9acb-102">Tipi obsoleti in .NET Framework</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e9acb-102">Obsolete Types in the .NET Framework</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="e9acb-103"><a name="introduction"></a> Le tabelle in questo articolo elencano i tipi obsoleti in [!INCLUDE[net_v45](../../../includes/net-v45-md.md)] e [!INCLUDE[net_v46](../../../includes/net-v46-md.md)], organizzati per assembly.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e9acb-103"><a name="introduction"></a> The tables in this article list the types that are obsolete in the [!INCLUDE[net_v45](../../../includes/net-v45-md.md)] and the [!INCLUDE[net_v46](../../../includes/net-v46-md.md)], organized by assembly.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e9acb-104">Usare i seguenti collegamenti per vedere un elenco di tipi obsoleti e le alternative consigliate in ogni assembly.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e9acb-104">Use the following links to see a list of the obsolete types and the recommended alternatives in each assembly.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e9acb-105">Poiché questi tipi sono obsoleti, lo sono anche tutti i relativi membri.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e9acb-105">Because these types are obsolete, all their members are also obsolete.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e9acb-106">Per un elenco di altri membri obsoleti nella libreria di classi .NET Framework, vedere [Membri obsoleti](../../../docs/framework/whats-new/obsolete-members.md).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e9acb-106">For a list of additional obsolete members in the .NET Framework class library, see [Obsolete Members](../../../docs/framework/whats-new/obsolete-members.md).</span></span>

<a name="obsolete_types_in_system_assemblies"></a>   
## <a name="obsolete-types-in-system-assemblies"></a><span data-ttu-id="e9acb-133">Tipi obsoleti negli assembly di sistema</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e9acb-133">Obsolete Types in System Assemblies</span></span>  
 <span data-ttu-id="e9acb-134">Nelle seguenti tabelle sono elencati i tipi dichiarati obsoleti negli assembly di sistema.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e9acb-134">The following tables list the types that have been declared obsolete in system assemblies.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e9acb-135">Questi assembly vengono usati per lo sviluppo di applicazioni generiche destinate a .NET Framework.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e9acb-135">These assemblies are used for general\-purpose application development that targets the .NET Framework.</span></span>

<a name="obsolete_types_in_microsoft_assemblies"></a>   
## <a name="obsolete-types-in-microsoft-assemblies"></a><span data-ttu-id="e9acb-925">Tipi obsoleti negli assembly Microsoft</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e9acb-925">Obsolete Types in Microsoft Assemblies</span></span>  
 <span data-ttu-id="e9acb-926">Nelle seguenti sezioni sono elencati i tipi obsoleti contenuti negli assembly Microsoft.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e9acb-926">The following sections list the obsolete types in Microsoft assemblies.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e9acb-927">Questi ultimi sono assembly speciali, ad esempio assembly destinati a un unico linguaggio (es. Microsoft.JScript.dll o Microsoft.VisualC.dll).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e9acb-927">These assemblies are special-purpose assemblies such as assemblies that target an individual language (for example, Microsoft.JScript.dll or Microsoft.VisualC.dll).</span></span>  
  
<a name="IEHost"></a>   
### <a name="assembly-iehostdll-and-ieexecexe"></a><span data-ttu-id="e9acb-928">Assembly: IEHost.dll e IEExec.exe</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e9acb-928">Assembly: IEHost.dll and IEExec.exe</span></span>  
 <span data-ttu-id="e9acb-929">Gli assembly IEHost.dll e IEExec.dll sono stati rimossi da .NET Framework.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e9acb-929">The IEHost.dll and IEExec.exe assemblies have been removed from the .NET Framework.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e9acb-930">Tutti i loro tipi e i membri sono obsoleti e non sono supportati da [!INCLUDE[net_v40_short](../../../includes/net-v40-short-md.md)].</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e9acb-930">All of their types and their members are obsolete and are not supported as of the [!INCLUDE[net_v40_short](../../../includes/net-v40-short-md.md)].</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e9acb-931">Questi assembly sono usati per eseguire l'hosting dei controlli Windows Form ed eseguire i file eseguibili in Internet Explorer.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e9acb-931">These assemblies were used to host Windows Forms controls and to run executables in Internet Explorer.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e9acb-932">Le alternative consigliate includono ClickOnce, le applicazioni browser XAML (XBAP) e Microsoft Silverlight.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e9acb-932">Recommended alternatives include ClickOnce, XAML browser applications (XBAP), and Microsoft Silverlight.</span></span>
